 Viju Khote was the brother of Bollywood's famous actress Shubha Khote
 Actor Viju Khote, best known for his roles in Sholay and Andaz Apna Apna, passed away on Monday
 He was 77
 
 After making his silver screen debut in 1964 film Ya Malak, Viju went on to star in movies like Sholay, Qurbani, Karz, Nagina, Qayamat Se Qayamat Tak and Andaz Apna Apna among more
 
 Viju Khote is best remembered for his brief role in Sholay, in which he played an underling of Amjad Khan's Gabbar
 His character in the film spoke one of the most well-known lines in Hindi cinema: "sardar maine aap ka namak khaya hai
 "
 In Andaz Apna Apna, he played the role of Robert and his appearance was also marked by a line of dialogue that later became famous: "galti se mistake hogaya
 "
 He was also known for his work in popular 90s sitcom Zabaan Sambhalke, which was based on British show Mind Your Language
 
 Besides having over 300 Hindi and Marathi films to his credit, Viju Khote was also active in Marathi theatre
 (via Indian Express)

 songdo ko honkong, singapore kii tarah finans city bananaa he
 Everything here is automatic
 ek centre se aap kisi bhi imaarat kaa taapmaana yaa urja kii khapat niyantrit kar sakate hai
 You will get a message on the mobile from the sensor that when the bus is about to arrive, type the problem on the mobile, the local administration will know
 isi se bharat ke sandarbh main sawaal uthta he ki kya iske liye hamaari sarkarein nagarpalika ke prashasan or adhikaron main bhi badlaav karegi
 In September 2013, BBC and a year later in November 2014, Financial Express wrote that not even 20 percent of Songdo's commercial space has been used
 abhi kya sthiti he aapke ankar ko nahin maaloom
 The comments songdo kii tarah bharat main ek finans city kaa ek charan banakar taiyaar ho gaya he
 In 2007, as the Chief Minister, Narendra Modi laid the foundation for it which will be completed in 2022 and till its completion it will take about 8 xxrep 4 0 crores
 jitna main samaj sakaa hum uske anusaar gujarat sarkaar ne banzar bhoomi lekar mumbai kii ek company se saajhedaari kii or ek nai company bana lee
 The new company raised capital loans of more than 1000 crores and created a structure
 gift bhi songdo kii tarah he
 There is a centrally cooling plant through which the temperature of all buildings will be controlled
 urja kii baari bachat hogi
 Similarly, the waste of all the buildings will be passed from the basement through a pipe to the Central Waste Management Plant
 sadakon ke bagal main underground tunnel bana he jisamen bijli, pani, kachra or asi ke liye thandi hawa le jane kii alag-alag pipe hai
 China has also built many such smart cities
 gaanv ke gaanv zameendos kar diye gaye smart city ke liye magar ab vahaan rahane vaala koi nahin
 Made so many cities so fast that most of the smart cities are empty
 in smarton kaa ab naam badal gaya he
 They are being called Ghost or City
 kya nahin he vahaan, bas aadmi nahin he
 On the basis of technology, the city's capacity will be developed, but will the city remain a city? bahut saare sawaal hai smart city ko lekar
 There are political questions as well as economic ones
 2005 main jeenyuarem shuru hui thi jiske tahat shaharon ke buniyadi dhaanchon main sudhaar karne kaa lakshya tay kiya gaya tha
 Good work has been done in many places but in many places money has been made in the name of work
 2012 main sieji ne report di thi ki jeenyuaram ke tahat manzur 1298 yojanaon main se 231 hi puri hui hai
 Under this scheme, a budget of more than 65 thousand crores was given, but the government did not release more than half the money
 nai amrit yojana ke tahat har rajya main kam se kam ek smart shahar hoga
 The city or place where the name will come in the smart city will get 100 crores every year for five years
 puri duniya main bahes he ki smart city kya he or kiske liye he
 Smart cities have also been prepared in China, Korea and Saudi and in many countries like Rio de Janeiro, old cities of Madrid type are being smartened
 2008 main ibiem company ne smart city kii avadharana viksit kii thi lekin ab kai ai or finans companiyaan smart city banane main shaamil hai
 This smart city will not be made with Make in India but with the help of foreign companies
 is janvari jab america ke raashtrapati obama bharat aae to yah qaraar hua ki america bharat main teen shaharon ko smart banane main madad karegaa
 Will help build three smart cities
 elahabaad, ajmer or vishakhapatnam
 In the budget for 2014-15, while deciding the amount of about 7000 crores of smart cities, it was said that smart cities will settle like satellites of big cities
 jaise mumbai ke paas navi mumbai he or dilli ke paas greater noida
 In this way, many multi-national companies are now engaged in the task of building smart cities
 hamaare desi real estate waalon ko mauka milegaa yaa nahin yah sab baad main pataa chalegaa
 The smart city scheme was launched at Kochi in Kerala, Ahmedabad in Gujarat, Aurangabad in Maharashtra, Manesar in Haryana, Kushkera in Rajasthan, Krishnapatna in Andhra Pradesh, Ponneri in Tamil Nadu and Tumkur in Karnataka during the UPA government
 2012 main kamalnath ne elaan kiya tha ki har rajya main do smart city banaaenge
 For this, UPA had fixed 18500 crore in the 2013 budget for smart city under JNNURM
 do saal main upie kya kar pai pataa nahin lekin ab pradhanmantri modi 100 smart city banane kii yojana par aage badhane ja rahe hai
 The government is preparing to make villages digital on one hand and on the other side is making digital cities for those coming from village to city
 ye saare log jo bharat kii shahari aabaadi ko 70 fisadi kar denge mobile sensor ke zariye smart city main rahane yogya honge yaa nahin ye sawaal to kisi raajnneetik dal ko poochna chahie
 The city is a subject in itself
 isaki padhai karne vaale vidwaan puch rahe hai ki dilli, mumbai main sattar fisadi log ausat aay vaale hote hai yaa garib hote hai
 Most people set up their shops in the corners of the streets, licking on the tracks, selling cinnamon almonds, selling shoes on the bonnet of a Maruti car under a tree, and the bells in the summer days, in winter They live by selling eggs
 kya in logon ke liye smart city main koi jagah hogi
 No one knows about it properly nor has our political parties made any sense on it
 vaise hamaare buildergan har saal is tarah kii city launch karte rahete hai
 Now these private cities with a population of twenty-five thousand have started being built from the police station to the school
 aapane dekha hoga ki bilderon kii city ke baahar kapadaa press karne vaala se lekar sabji vaala dukaan lagaakar pet paalataa he
 Will he get a chance in the smart city? kya maujuuda shahar ek had se zyada behatar nahin ho sakate
 By the way, many old cities of the world have built projects of 20 to 50 million dollars to better themselves

 Ratan Tata, who is going to hand over the reins of the country's largest industrial house to his successor Cyrus Mistry on Friday, is not only leaving a huge $ 100 billion business empire for him, but he is also leaving a legacy, due to which the business world He has a special identity
 1971 main ratan tata ko rashtriya radio or electronics company limited (nelco) kaa director-in-charge niyukt kiya gaya, ek company jo ki sakht vittiya kathinaayee kii sthiti main thi
 Ratan suggested that the company should invest in the development of high-technology products rather than consumer electronics
 JRD was reluctant because of Nelco's historical financial performance, as it had never paid regular dividends before
 iske alaava, jab ratan tata ne kaary bhaar sambhala, upabhokta electronics nelco kii bazaar main hissedari 2% thi, or ghaataa bikri kaa 40% tha
 Nevertheless, JRD followed Ratan's suggestion
 1972 se 1975 tak, antat nelco ne apni bazaar main hissedari 20% tak badha lee or apana ghaataa bhi puraa kar liya
 But in 1975, Indira Gandhi, the Prime Minister of India, declared a state of emergency, which led to the economic recession
 iske baad 1977 main union kii samasyayen huin, isliye maang ke bad jane par bhi utpaadan main sudhaar nahin ho paaya
 Eventually, Tata faced a union strike, locked out for seven months
 ratan tata ne hameshaa nelco kii moulik dridhtaa main vishvas rakhaa, lekin udhyam aage or na rah sakaa
 In the year 1981, Ratan was made the chairman of Tata Industries and other holding companies of the group, where he was responsible for transforming the group's strategic idea group and promoter of new ventures into high technology businesses
 1991 main unhone jearady se group chair main kaa kaary bhaar sambhala
 The Tatas removed the old guards and the young managers were given responsibilities
 tab se lekar, unhone, tata group ke aakaar ko hi badal diya he, jo aaj bhartiya share bazaar main kisi bhi anya vyapaarik udhyam se adhik bazaar puunji rakhata he
 Under Ratan's guidance, Tata Consultancy Services became a public corporation and Tata Motors was listed on the New York Stock Exchange
 1998 main tata motors ne unke sankalpit tata indica ko bazaar main utaara
 On 31 January 2007, under the chairmanship of Ratan Tata, Tata Sons successfully acquired the Corus Group, an anglo-dutch aluminum and steel manufacturer
 is adhigrahan ke saath ratan tata bhartiya vyapaar jagat main ek pratishthit vyakti ban gayi
 As a result of this merger, the world got the fifth largest steel producing institution
